***fulcrum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a> (45502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bedpost, foot of a couch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fulciō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prop up, support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fulcrums</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fulcra</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:mechanics.html>mechanics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The support about which a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> pivots.
<dl><dd><i>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possible to flick food across the table using your fork as a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> and your finger as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Allison_(artist)" class="extiw" title="w:John Allison (artist)">John Allison</a>, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scarygoround.com/?date=20100126">Bad Machinery</a></i>
<dl><dd>MILDRED: Archimedes <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> long enough and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> on which to place it and I will move the world.</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:charlotte.html>Charlotte</a>: Yeah she <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> that twaddle eight or nine times.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> March 1,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Petroski" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Petroski"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Petroski</a>,  “Opening Doors”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="w:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/pub/opening-doors">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 2, page 112-3:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A doorknob of whatever roundish shape <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> effectively a continuum of <a href = vnd.unilang:levers.html>levers</a>, with the axis of the latching mechanism | known as the spindle | being the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> about which the turning <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> place.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crux or pivot; a central point.
<ul><li><b>2006</b>, Rebecca Langlands, <i>Sexual Morality in Ancient <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a></i> (page 119)
<dl><dd>By this point the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> of concern <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the <i>stuprum</i> of <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> upon <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>, described as more prevalent than that upon women.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***fuller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> (9733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i></span></span>: more <span class="Latn" lang="en">full</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, from the verb.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who fulls cloth.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">walker</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">waulker</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a>'s earth</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a>'s herb</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a>'s thistle</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a>'s weed</span></li></ul>
</div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/220px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/330px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/440px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="960" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Sword blade with <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> along the centre.</div></div></div>
<p>Unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A convex, rounded or grooved tool, used by blacksmiths for shaping metal.</li>
<li>A groove made by such a tool (in the blade of a sword etc.).</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fullering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fullered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form a groove or channel in, by a <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> or set hammer.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></b> a bayonet</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***functie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functie</a> (4680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fonction</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">function</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">functiō</i>. The spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> eventually adapted to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">functiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:functies.html>functies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:functie.html>functietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>job, position</li>
<li>function, purpose</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> function</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> function</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> function</li>
<li>use, purpose (of a machine or tool)</li></ol>

***futuristisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:futuristisch.html>futuristisch</a> (49524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:futurist.html>futurist</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-isch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:futuristisch.html>futuristisch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:futuristischer.html>futuristischer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:futuristisch.html>futuristisch</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">futuristischt</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>futuristic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">resembling something from the distant future; resembling <a href = vnd.unilang:science-fiction.html>science-fiction</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> fantastically future-like</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from mid 20th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> futuristic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pertaining to futurism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 1910s]</span></li></ol>

***gaai.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a> (47413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:gai.html>gai</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gaius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Further etymology uncertain, though plausibly echoic, and supposedly influenced by the Roman common given name <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Gaius</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaaien.html>gaaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:jaybird.html>jaybird</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Garrulus_glandarinus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Garrulus glandarinus"><i>Garrulus glandarinus</i></a></span>, a woodland corvine species</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">Vlaamse <a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A parallel form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">papagaai</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">parrot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, by popular etymology confused with etymology 1, but actually from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">papagoie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">papegoie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بَبَّغَاء</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">babbaḡāʾ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بپغا</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bapğâ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaaien.html>gaaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wooden, somewhat bird-shaped target, often ornamented with bright plumes, used in archery competitions</li>
<li>The high wooden <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a> or tower the above <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mounted on</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>(wooden base) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wip.html>wip</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schutsboom</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gaaischieten</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">verb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gaaischieter</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gaaischieting</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A parallel form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gade.html>gade</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaaien.html>gaaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">gaaike</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A female spouse, notably (and mostly used in the diminutive):
<ol><li>a female bird</li>
<li>a female fish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a human mistress or wife</li></ol></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijfje.html>wijfje</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***gaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> (64)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gān</i>, from a fusion of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gāną</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganganą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰeh₁-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰengʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go, to move from one place to another
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm <b>going</b> to the beach.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nergens.html>nergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naartoe.html>naartoe</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That car isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>going</b> anywhere.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave or depart, to move away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They're <b>leaving</b> again tomorrow.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lead (in a direction)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Limburg.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This road <b>goes</b> all the way to Limburg.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to proceed (well or poorly)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a></b> well.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it <b>going</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>work</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms the future tense of a verb, similarly to English going to future tense</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not going</b> to work anyway.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to, begin to, to be going to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schijnen.html>schijnen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The sun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>starting to</b> shine again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slapen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm <b>going</b> to sleep.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's <b>going to</b> start raining soon.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used for the future tense, but <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> more formal</li>
<li>In questions, the past tense <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>)</i> in the sense of “to go” can be used to indicate the present. In Dutch, one can ask “Ging <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verjaardag.html>verjaardag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?” which means “<b>Are</b> you still <b>going</b> to that birthday party tonight?”. The question implies there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a plan to go to the <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> party, and asks for confirmation that the plan <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still on. This exceptional use of the past tense with a present meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also seen for the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gaer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ready</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">garo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ready</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*garwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ready</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***gab.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gab.html>gab</a> (36120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gabben</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gabban</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scoff, mock, delude, jest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">gabba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mock, make sport of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gabbaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mock, jest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ghabh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be split, be forked, <a href = vnd.unilang:gapen.html>gape</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:gab.html>gab</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mock, <a href = vnd.unilang:prate.html>prate</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:North Frisian language">North Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frr">gabben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to jest, sport</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gabben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">gabben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to jest, have fun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gab.html>gab</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gabs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Idle chatter.</li>
<li>The mouth or gob.</li>
<li>One of the open-forked <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> of rods controlling reversing in early steam engines.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:talkative</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">begab</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gabby.html>gabby</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gift of the <a href = vnd.unilang:gab.html>gab</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gab.html>gab</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gabs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gabbing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gabbed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To jest; to tell lies in jest; exaggerate; lie.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To talk or chatter a lot, usually on trivial <a href = vnd.unilang:subjects.html>subjects</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To speak or tell falsely.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gade.html>gade</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gegade</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gigado</i>. Substantivised form of the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gade.html>gaden</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now obsolete. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gatte</i>.

***gaffel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaffel.html>gaffel</a> (93369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gaffele</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaffel.html>gaffel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaffel.html>gaffels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaffel.html>gaffeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A two-pronged pitchfork or bident.</li>
<li>Any two-pronged fork, such as a carving fork.</li>
<li>A two-pronged antler of a two-years old stag.</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">galge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*galga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galgô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰalgʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰalg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">long switch, rod, shaft, pole, perch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:galgen.html>Galgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">galge</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gallows</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">galge</i>.

***gallisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a> (130945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">חלש</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khallish</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nauseous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חַלָשׁ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chalash</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>Said</a> to be used in theatre circles originally. Probably an association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geil.html>geil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gallig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">choleric</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> made, whence the senses <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">angry</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hot</i>, an instance of folk etymology.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>nauseous</li>
<li>angry, irritated</li>
<li>hot, sensuous, <a href = vnd.unilang:horny.html>horny</a></li></ol>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> word <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gallisch.html>gallisch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
